`pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go` with a precedence hierarchy (Viewer:20, Editor:30, Admin:40) implemented via the `rolePrecedence` map and `Includes()` method. The `RoleType` interface enforces that higher roles include permissions of lower roles. These roles are assigned to organization users in `pkg/services/org/model.go` via the `OrgUser` struct.\\n\\n## Role-to-Permission Mapping\\nPermission grants are centrally declared in `pkg/api/accesscontrol.go` via the `declareFixedRoles()` function, which creates `RoleRegistration` entries that map org roles (RoleViewer, RoleEditor, RoleAdmin) to fixed roles with specific permissions. For example, datasources:explorer is granted to RoleEditor and optionally RoleViewer. The `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go` file defines additional role mappings for org users management and other features.\\n\\n## Permission Guard Middleware\\nRequest-level permission enforcement is handled by `pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`, which implements the `Middleware()` function that wraps HTTP handlers. The `authorize()` function evaluates permissions using the AccessControl service, checking whether a user has required permissions via scope-based evaluation. The `pkg/services/accesscontrol/evaluator.go` and `pkg/services/accesscontrol/checker.go` provide the evaluation logic.\\n\\n## Dashboard and Folder Permissions\\nDashboard and folder permissions are managed through dedicated API endpoints in `pkg/api/dashboard_permission.go` and `pkg/api/folder_permission.go`. These endpoints handle both getting and updating permissions for specific resources.\\n\\n## Permission Inheritance\\nFolder and dashboard permission inheritance is implemented through scope resolution in `pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go`. The `GetInheritedScopes()` function retrieves parent folder scopes to support inherited permissions, while `NewFolderUIDScopeResolver()` and `NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver()` create scope resolvers that include parent folder scopes. The folder service in `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go` provides the `GetParents()` method that retrieves the folder hierarchy for permission inheritance.\\n\\n## Resource Permission Management\\nThe `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/` package provides services for managing resource-level permissions, with the `service.go` handling permission operations and `store.go` persisting permissions to the database.
